a.id,
a.cus_no,
a.cus_name,
a.cus_sname,
a.cus_lastid AS cus_lastname,
a.cus_tel,
a.cus_city,
a.cus_address,
a.cus_note,
(
SELECT cc.con_name
FROM T_cus_con cc
WHERE id = a.con_id
) AS con_name,
(SELECT u.user_tname FROM t_sys_user AS u WHERE u.id=a.user_id) as user_name,
(
SELECT STUFF((SELECT ','+u2.user_tname FROM t_sys_user AS u2 WHERE CHARINDEX(CAST(u2.id as VARCHAR),a.con_team) >0 FOR XML PATH ('')),1,1,'')
)
as con_team,
a.con_is_pub,
a.con_back,
a.cus_createTime,
b.*
FROM T_cus_base AS a
INNER JOIN T_cus_expvalue_10000 AS b ON a.id = b.cus_id WHERE con_back=0 AND (user_id=3 OR con_is_pub=1)) AS T

a.id,
a.cus_no,
a.cus_name,

a.cus_lastid AS cus_lastname,
a.cus_tel,
a.cus_city,
a.cus_address,
a.cus_note,
(
SELECT cc.con_name
FROM T_cus_con cc
WHERE id = a.con_id
) AS con_name,
(SELECT u.user_tname FROM t_sys_user AS u WHERE u.id=a.user_id) as user_name,
(
SELECT STUFF((SELECT ','+u2.user_tname FROM t_sys_user AS u2 WHERE CHARINDEX(CAST(u2.id as VARCHAR),a.con_team) >0 FOR XML PATH ('')),1,1,'')
)
as con_team,
a.con_is_pub,
a.con_back,
a.cus_createTime,
b.*
FROM T_cus_base AS a
INNER JOIN T_cus_expvalue_10000 AS b ON a.id = b.cus_id WHERE con_back=0 AND (user_id=3 OR con_is_pub=1)) AS T

a.cus_createTime,

FROM T_cus_base AS a
